ACL Authorization Code Audit\\n\\n### Summary\\nFound comprehensive ACL authorization implementation in Apache Kafka spanning across core, clients, metadata, and server modules. The authorization architecture includes the main Authorizer interface, a ClusterMetadataAuthorizer extension, the StandardAuthorizer implementation, and supporting infrastructure for ACL management.\\n\\n### Core Architecture\\n\\n**Main Interface Definition:**\\n- **Authorizer.java** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/authorizer/): Defines the pluggable authorizer interface for Kafka brokers. This is the primary interface that all authorizer implementations must implement. It includes methods for:\\n  - start(AuthorizerServerInfo): Initialize the authorizer\\n  - authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List<Action>): Perform authorization checks\\n  - createAcls/deleteAcls: Manage ACL bindings\\n  - acls(AclBindingFilter): Query ACL bindings\\n  - authorizeByResourceType: Default method for checking authorization by resource type\\n\\n**Extended Interface:**\\n- **ClusterMetadataAuthorizer.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/): Extends Authorizer for authorizers that store state in the __cluster_metadata log. Includes additional methods:\\n  - setAclMutator/aclMutatorOrException: Manage the ACL mutator\\n  - completeInitialLoad: Signal completion of initial load\\n  - loadSnapshot: Load ACLs from snapshot\\n  - addAcl/removeAcl: Manage ACLs directly\\n\\n**Built-in Implementation:**\\n- **StandardAuthorizer.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/): Concrete implementation of ClusterMetadataAuthorizer. This is the modern, built-in authorizer that stores ACLs in the cluster metadata log. Implements the Monitorable interface for metrics support.\\n\\n**Server Info Implementation:**\\n- **KafkaAuthorizerServerInfo.java** (server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/network/): Concrete implementation of AuthorizerServerInfo interface providing runtime broker configuration metadata to authorizers during startup.\\n\\n### Supporting Interfaces\\n\\n**Request Context & Metadata:**\\n- **AuthorizerServerInfo.java** (clients/src/main/java): Interface for runtime broker configuration metadata including cluster resource, broker ID, endpoints, inter-broker endpoint, and early start listeners.\\n- **AuthorizableRequestContext.java** (clients/src/main/java): Interface providing request context data including listener name, security protocol, principal, client address, request type/version/ID, and correlation ID.\\n\\n**Authorization Models:**\\n- **Action.java** (clients/src/main/java): Class representing an action being authorized with resource pattern, operation, reference count, and logging flags.\\n- **AuthorizationResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Enum with ALLOWED and DENIED states for authorization decisions.\\n\\n**Result Classes:**\\n- **AclCreateResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Result class for ACL creation operations with optional exception.\\n- **AclDeleteResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Result class for ACL deletion operations with exception and binding delete results.\\n\\n### Metadata and Data Management\\n\\n**ACL Storage Interfaces:**\\n- **AclMutator.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Interface implemented by QuorumController for ACL create and delete operations in ClusterMetadataAuthorizer instances.\\n\\n**Data Classes:**\\n- **StandardAcl.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Represents a Kafka ACL identified by UUID and stored in metadata log.\\n- **StandardAuthorizerData.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Immutable class holding ACL data for KRaft-based clusters.\\n- **AclCache.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Immutable cache storing ACLs sorted by resource and indexed by UUID.\\n- **StandardAclRecordIterator.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Iterator for batch retrieval of ACL records.\\n- **StandardAclWithId.java** (metadata/src/main/java): ACL representation with associated UUID.\\n\\n**ACL Publisher:**\\n- **AclPublisher.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/publisher/): Handles ACL updates from metadata snapshots and incremental changes, notifying ClusterMetadataAuthorizer instances.\\n\\n### Utility Classes\\n\\n**Authorization Utilities:**\\n- **AuthorizerUtils.java** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/): Utility class for creating and wrapping authorizer instances with metrics. Contains createAuthorizer() method.\\n- **AclEntry.java** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/): Utility class providing ACL constants and helper methods including:\\n  - Wildcard definitions for principals and hosts\\n  - supportedOperations(ResourceType): Returns valid operations per resource type\\n  - authorizationError(ResourceType): Maps resource types to error codes\\n\\n**Exception:**\\n- **AuthorizerNotReadyException.java** (clients/src/main/java): RetriableException indicating the authorizer is not yet ready to process requests.\\n\\n### Test Utilities\\n\\n**Test Implementation:**\\n- **MonitorableAuthorizer** (in AuthorizerUtilsTest.java, server/src/test/java): Test utility implementing Authorizer and Monitorable for testing metrics integration. Demonstrates how to implement both interfaces.\\n\\n### File Organization Summary\\n\\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/authorizer/**: Public API interfaces (Authorizer, AuthorizerServerInfo, AuthorizableRequestContext) and supporting classes (Action, AuthorizationResult, AclCreateResult, AclDeleteResult)\\n- **metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/**: KRaft-based authorization implementation (ClusterMetadataAuthorizer, StandardAuthorizer, StandardAcl, AclMutator, AclCache, StandardAuthorizerData, supporting classes)\\n- **server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/**: Server-side utilities (AuthorizerUtils, AclEntry)\\n- **server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/network/**: KafkaAuthorizerServerInfo implementation\\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/errors/**: AuthorizerNotReadyException\\n\\n### Authorization Flow\\n\\n1. Broker creates authorizer instance from configured class name (AuthorizerUtils.createAuthorizer)\\n2. Broker calls authorizer.start() with server metadata\\n3. For KRaft-based clusters, StandardAuthorizer loads initial ACLs from metadata snapshot\\n4. ACLPublisher updates authorizer as ACLs change in cluster metadata\\n5. For each request, broker calls authorize() with action list\\n6. StandardAuthorizer consults cached ACLs to make authorization decisions\\n7. ACL Authorization Code Audit\\n\\n### Summary\\nFound comprehensive ACL authorization implementation in Apache Kafka spanning across core, clients, metadata, and server modules. The authorization architecture includes the main Authorizer interface, a ClusterMetadataAuthorizer extension, the StandardAuthorizer implementation, and supporting infrastructure for ACL management.\\n\\n### Core Architecture\\n\\n**Main Interface Definition:**\\n- **Authorizer.java** (clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/authorizer/): Defines the pluggable authorizer interface for Kafka brokers. This is the primary interface that all authorizer implementations must implement. It includes methods for:\\n  - start(AuthorizerServerInfo): Initialize the authorizer\\n  - authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List<Action>): Perform authorization checks\\n  - createAcls/deleteAcls: Manage ACL bindings\\n  - acls(AclBindingFilter): Query ACL bindings\\n  - authorizeByResourceType: Default method for checking authorization by resource type\\n\\n**Extended Interface:**\\n- **ClusterMetadataAuthorizer.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/): Extends Authorizer for authorizers that store state in the __cluster_metadata log. Includes additional methods:\\n  - setAclMutator/aclMutatorOrException: Manage the ACL mutator\\n  - completeInitialLoad: Signal completion of initial load\\n  - loadSnapshot: Load ACLs from snapshot\\n  - addAcl/removeAcl: Manage ACLs directly\\n\\n**Built-in Implementation:**\\n- **StandardAuthorizer.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/): Concrete implementation of ClusterMetadataAuthorizer. This is the modern, built-in authorizer that stores ACLs in the cluster metadata log. Implements the Monitorable interface for metrics support.\\n\\n**Server Info Implementation:**\\n- **KafkaAuthorizerServerInfo.java** (server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/network/): Concrete implementation of AuthorizerServerInfo interface providing runtime broker configuration metadata to authorizers during startup.\\n\\n### Supporting Interfaces\\n\\n**Request Context & Metadata:**\\n- **AuthorizerServerInfo.java** (clients/src/main/java): Interface for runtime broker configuration metadata including cluster resource, broker ID, endpoints, inter-broker endpoint, and early start listeners.\\n- **AuthorizableRequestContext.java** (clients/src/main/java): Interface providing request context data including listener name, security protocol, principal, client address, request type/version/ID, and correlation ID.\\n\\n**Authorization Models:**\\n- **Action.java** (clients/src/main/java): Class representing an action being authorized with resource pattern, operation, reference count, and logging flags.\\n- **AuthorizationResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Enum with ALLOWED and DENIED states for authorization decisions.\\n\\n**Result Classes:**\\n- **AclCreateResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Result class for ACL creation operations with optional exception.\\n- **AclDeleteResult.java** (clients/src/main/java): Result class for ACL deletion operations with exception and binding delete results.\\n\\n### Metadata and Data Management\\n\\n**ACL Storage Interfaces:**\\n- **AclMutator.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Interface implemented by QuorumController for ACL create and delete operations in ClusterMetadataAuthorizer instances.\\n\\n**Data Classes:**\\n- **StandardAcl.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Represents a Kafka ACL identified by UUID and stored in metadata log.\\n- **StandardAuthorizerData.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Immutable class holding ACL data for KRaft-based clusters.\\n- **AclCache.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Immutable cache storing ACLs sorted by resource and indexed by UUID.\\n- **StandardAclRecordIterator.java** (metadata/src/main/java): Iterator for batch retrieval of ACL records.\\n- **StandardAclWithId.java** (metadata/src/main/java): ACL representation with associated UUID.\\n\\n**ACL Publisher:**\\n- **AclPublisher.java** (metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/publisher/): Handles ACL updates from metadata snapshots and incremental changes, notifying ClusterMetadataAuthorizer instances.\\n\\n### Utility Classes\\n\\n**Authorization Utilities:**\\n- **AuthorizerUtils.java** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/): Utility class for creating and wrapping authorizer instances with metrics. Contains createAuthorizer() method.\\n- **AclEntry.java** (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/): Utility class providing ACL constants and helper methods including:\\n  - Wildcard definitions for principals and hosts\\n  - supportedOperations(ResourceType): Returns valid operations per resource type\\n  - authorizationError(ResourceType): Maps resource types to error codes\\n\\n**Exception:**\\n- **AuthorizerNotReadyException.java** (clients/src/main/java): RetriableException indicating the authorizer is not yet ready to process requests.\\n\\n### Test Utilities\\n\\n**Test Implementation:**\\n- **MonitorableAuthorizer** (in AuthorizerUtilsTest.java, server/src/test/java): Test utility implementing Authorizer and Monitorable for testing metrics integration. Demonstrates how to implement both interfaces.\\n\\n### File Organization Summary\\n\\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/authorizer/**: Public API interfaces (Authorizer, AuthorizerServerInfo, AuthorizableRequestContext) and supporting classes (Action, AuthorizationResult, AclCreateResult, AclDeleteResult)\\n- **metadata/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/metadata/authorizer/**: KRaft-based authorization implementation (ClusterMetadataAuthorizer, StandardAuthorizer, StandardAcl, AclMutator, AclCache, StandardAuthorizerData, supporting classes)\\n- **server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/security/authorizer/**: Server-side utilities (AuthorizerUtils, AclEntry)\\n- **server-common/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/network/**: KafkaAuthorizerServerInfo implementation\\n- **clients/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/common/errors/**: AuthorizerNotReadyException\\n\\n### Authorization Flow\\n\\n1. Broker creates authorizer instance from configured class name (AuthorizerUtils.createAuthorizer)\\n2. Broker calls authorizer.start() with server metadata\\n3. For KRaft-based clusters, StandardAuthorizer loads initial ACLs from metadata snapshot\\n4. ACLPublisher updates authorizer as ACLs change in cluster metadata\\n5. For each request, broker calls authorize() with action list\\n6. StandardAuthorizer consults cached ACLs to make authorization decisions\\n7. ACL mutations go through AclMutator interface to QuorumController\\n\\nAll code is located in the github.com/sg-evals/kafka--0753c489 repository across multiple modules.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
